    Task

    Exploring AnyParser Features

    As a potential customer, I explore the different document parsing features of AnyParser, so that I can determine which solutions best meet my needs for content extraction.

    Success definition: Given I am on the AnyParser main page in the sandbox environment When I click on the 'Try Sandbox' button and subsequently interact with the 'Full Content' and 'Table Only' buttons Then I should see detailed descriptions and functionalities of full content and table extraction, including instructions for processing files and downloading results in various formats.

    heading AnyParser's Capabilities
    heading
    StaticText Privacy Protection: Activate the "Remove Private Information" feature, and AnyParser will automatically redact P.I.I. during the document extraction.
    StaticText You can instruct the model to include or omit page numbers, headers, footers, figures, charts, etc.
    StaticText AnyParser doesn’t just extract text and tables, it also retrieves figures, charts, and footnotes packed with vital information 2X faster and 5X more cost efficient
    StaticText Bid farewell to jumbled tables and chaotic layouts that plague traditional OCR-based models with a 2X more precision and 2.5X more recall than industry average.

    Reasoning for action: Clicking on the 'Try Sandbox' button is the initial step necessary to engage with AnyParser's features relevant to document parsing.     Action: click(64) # Click on the 'Try Sandbox' button to explore the sandbox feature of AnyParser.
